# Unicode Hex Input — keyboard layout reference

Generated by keylayout_to_xkb. Physical key labels use the US-QWERTY position; for a layout that is physically US-QWERTY the labels match the keycaps, otherwise read each key's Base output as the true legend.


**Keyboard-type variants:** primary, jis


## By-key summary


Quick reference: the four base planes for every character key, by keyboard row. Per-layer sections below add the caps planes, code points, and full descriptions.


**Number row**


| Key | Base | Shift | Option | Shift+Option |
|-----|------|-------|--------|--------------|
| Grave | `` ` `` | `~` |  |  |
| 1 | `1` | `!` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 2 | `2` | `@` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 3 | `3` | `#` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 4 | `4` | `$` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 5 | `5` | `%` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 6 | `6` | `^` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 7 | `7` | `&` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 8 | `8` | `*` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 9 | `9` | `(` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| 0 | `0` | `)` | ⟨dead⟩ | ⟨dead⟩ |
| Minus | `-` | `_` |  |  |
| Equal | `=` | `+` |  |  |

## Layer: Base (No Modifiers)


**Number row**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| Grave | `` ` `` | U+0060 | GRAVE ACCENT |
| 1 | `1` | U+0031 | DIGIT ONE |
| 2 | `2` | U+0032 | DIGIT TWO |
| 3 | `3` | U+0033 | DIGIT THREE |
| 4 | `4` | U+0034 | DIGIT FOUR |
| 5 | `5` | U+0035 | DIGIT FIVE |
| 6 | `6` | U+0036 | DIGIT SIX |
| 7 | `7` | U+0037 | DIGIT SEVEN |
| 8 | `8` | U+0038 | DIGIT EIGHT |
| 9 | `9` | U+0039 | DIGIT NINE |
| 0 | `0` | U+0030 | DIGIT ZERO |
| Minus | `-` | U+002D | HYPHEN-MINUS |
| Equal | `=` | U+003D | EQUALS SIGN |

**Top letter row (QWERTY)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| Q | `q` | U+0071 | LATIN SMALL LETTER Q |
| W | `w` | U+0077 | LATIN SMALL LETTER W |
| E | `e` | U+0065 | LATIN SMALL LETTER E |
| R | `r` | U+0072 | LATIN SMALL LETTER R |
| T | `t` | U+0074 | LATIN SMALL LETTER T |
| Y | `y` | U+0079 | LATIN SMALL LETTER Y |
| U | `u` | U+0075 | LATIN SMALL LETTER U |
| I | `i` | U+0069 | LATIN SMALL LETTER I |
| O | `o` | U+006F | LATIN SMALL LETTER O |
| P | `p` | U+0070 | LATIN SMALL LETTER P |
| LeftBracket | `[` | U+005B | LEFT SQUARE BRACKET |
| RightBracket | `]` | U+005D | RIGHT SQUARE BRACKET |
| Backslash | `\` | U+005C | REVERSE SOLIDUS |

**Home row (ASDF)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| A | `a` | U+0061 | LATIN SMALL LETTER A |
| S | `s` | U+0073 | LATIN SMALL LETTER S |
| D | `d` | U+0064 | LATIN SMALL LETTER D |
| F | `f` | U+0066 | LATIN SMALL LETTER F |
| G | `g` | U+0067 | LATIN SMALL LETTER G |
| H | `h` | U+0068 | LATIN SMALL LETTER H |
| J | `j` | U+006A | LATIN SMALL LETTER J |
| K | `k` | U+006B | LATIN SMALL LETTER K |
| L | `l` | U+006C | LATIN SMALL LETTER L |
| Semicolon | `;` | U+003B | SEMICOLON |
| Quote | `'` | U+0027 | APOSTROPHE |

**Bottom row (ZXCV)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| Z | `z` | U+007A | LATIN SMALL LETTER Z |
| X | `x` | U+0078 | LATIN SMALL LETTER X |
| C | `c` | U+0063 | LATIN SMALL LETTER C |
| V | `v` | U+0076 | LATIN SMALL LETTER V |
| B | `b` | U+0062 | LATIN SMALL LETTER B |
| N | `n` | U+006E | LATIN SMALL LETTER N |
| M | `m` | U+006D | LATIN SMALL LETTER M |
| Comma | `,` | U+002C | COMMA |
| Period | `.` | U+002E | FULL STOP |
| Slash | `/` | U+002F | SOLIDUS |
| Space | (space) | U+0020 | SPACE |

## Layer: Shift / Caps + Shift


(These modifier combinations produce identical output; they share one key table.)


**Number row**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| Grave | `~` | U+007E | TILDE |
| 1 | `!` | U+0021 | EXCLAMATION MARK |
| 2 | `@` | U+0040 | COMMERCIAL AT |
| 3 | `#` | U+0023 | NUMBER SIGN |
| 4 | `$` | U+0024 | DOLLAR SIGN |
| 5 | `%` | U+0025 | PERCENT SIGN |
| 6 | `^` | U+005E | CIRCUMFLEX ACCENT |
| 7 | `&` | U+0026 | AMPERSAND |
| 8 | `*` | U+002A | ASTERISK |
| 9 | `(` | U+0028 | LEFT PARENTHESIS |
| 0 | `)` | U+0029 | RIGHT PARENTHESIS |
| Minus | `_` | U+005F | LOW LINE |
| Equal | `+` | U+002B | PLUS SIGN |

**Top letter row (QWERTY)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| Q | `Q` | U+0051 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER Q |
| W | `W` | U+0057 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER W |
| E | `E` | U+0045 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER E |
| R | `R` | U+0052 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER R |
| T | `T` | U+0054 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER T |
| Y | `Y` | U+0059 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER Y |
| U | `U` | U+0055 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER U |
| I | `I` | U+0049 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER I |
| O | `O` | U+004F | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER O |
| P | `P` | U+0050 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER P |
| LeftBracket | `{` | U+007B | LEFT CURLY BRACKET |
| RightBracket | `}` | U+007D | RIGHT CURLY BRACKET |
| Backslash | `\|` | U+007C | VERTICAL LINE |

**Home row (ASDF)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| A | `A` | U+0041 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A |
| S | `S` | U+0053 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER S |
| D | `D` | U+0044 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER D |
| F | `F` | U+0046 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER F |
| G | `G` | U+0047 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER G |
| H | `H` | U+0048 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER H |
| J | `J` | U+004A | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER J |
| K | `K` | U+004B | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER K |
| L | `L` | U+004C | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER L |
| Semicolon | `:` | U+003A | COLON |
| Quote | `"` | U+0022 | QUOTATION MARK |

**Bottom row (ZXCV)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| Z | `Z` | U+005A | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER Z |
| X | `X` | U+0058 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER X |
| C | `C` | U+0043 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER C |
| V | `V` | U+0056 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER V |
| B | `B` | U+0042 | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER B |
| N | `N` | U+004E | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER N |
| M | `M` | U+004D | LATIN CAPITAL LETTER M |
| Comma | `<` | U+003C | LESS-THAN SIGN |
| Period | `>` | U+003E | GREATER-THAN SIGN |
| Slash | `?` | U+003F | QUESTION MARK |
| Space | (space) | U+0020 | SPACE |

## Layer: Option / Shift + Option / Caps + Option / Caps + Shift + Option


(These modifier combinations produce identical output; they share one key table.)


**Number row**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| 1 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 2 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 3 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 4 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 5 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 6 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 7 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 8 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 9 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| 0 | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |

**Top letter row (QWERTY)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| E | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |

**Home row (ASDF)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| A | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| D | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| F | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |

**Bottom row (ZXCV)**


| Key | Output | Code point | Description |
|-----|--------|-----------|-------------|
| C | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |
| B | ⟨dead key⟩ | | Dead key: Dead key |

## Dead keys


Each dead key composes with the next key pressed. A base key with no listed composition falls back to the dead key's accent character followed by the base character (for example, umlaut then `s` gives `¨s`).


### Dead key (reached by Option+0)


Standalone accent: `` (). 0 compositions.


| Base | Result | Code point | Description |
|------|--------|-----------|-------------|
